doctrine_mrsad_sins = {
	group = "mrsad_sins"
	number_of_picks = 12

	doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1 = {
		name = {
			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1_ingame_name
			}
		}
		desc = {
			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1_ingame_desc
			}
		}
		piety_cost = {
			value = faith_doctrine_cost_low
			subtract = 0
			if = {
				limit = { has_doctrine =  doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1 }
				multiply = faith_unchanged_doctrine_cost_mult
			}
		}
		is_shown = {
			always = yes
			NOT = { doctrine:doctrine_virtue_education_intrigue_1 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines } }
		}
		can_pick = {
			always = yes
		}
		traits = {
			sins = {
				education_intrigue_1 = { scale = 1 weight = 3 }
			}
		}
	} 

	doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1_strong = {
		name = {
			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1_strong_ingame_name
			}
		}
		desc = {
			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1_strong_ingame_desc
			}
		}
		piety_cost = {

			subtract = 0
			if = {
				limit = { has_doctrine =  doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1_strong }
				multiply = faith_unchanged_doctrine_cost_mult
			}
		}
		is_shown = {
			always = yes
			NOT = { doctrine:doctrine_virtue_education_intrigue_1_strong = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines } }
		}
		can_pick = {
			always = yes
			custom_description = {
				text = doctrine_requires_sin_trigger
				OR = {
					doctrine:doctrine_sin_education_intrigue_1 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
					doctrine:doctrine_sin_education_intrigue = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
				}
			}
		}
		traits = {
			sins = {
				education_intrigue_1 = { scale = 2 weight = 5 }
			}
		}
	}

			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_diplomatic_court_2_ingame_name
			}
		}
		desc = {
			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_diplomatic_court_2_ingame_desc
			}
		}
		piety_cost = {
			value = faith_doctrine_cost_low
			subtract = 0
			if = {
				limit = { has_doctrine =  doctrine_sin_diplomatic_court_2 }
				multiply = faith_unchanged_doctrine_cost_mult
			}
		}
		is_shown = {
			always = yes
			NOT = { doctrine:doctrine_virtue_diplomatic_court_2 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines } }
		}
		can_pick = {
			always = yes
		}
		traits = {
			sins = {
				diplomatic_court_2 = { scale = 1 weight = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_education_republican_knowledge_2_ingame_name
			}
		}
		desc = {
			first_valid = {
				desc = doctrine_sin_education_republican_knowledge_2_ingame_desc
			}
		}
		piety_cost = {
			value = faith_doctrine_cost_low
			subtract = 0
			if = {
				limit = { has_doctrine =  doctrine_sin_education_republican_knowledge_2 }
				multiply = faith_unchanged_doctrine_cost_mult
			}
		}
		is_shown = {
			always = yes
			NOT = { doctrine:doctrine_virtue_education_republican_knowledge_2 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines } }
		}
		can_pick = {
			always = yes
			custom_description = {
				text = doctrine_requires_sequential_traits_sin_trigger
				OR = {
					doctrine:doctrine_sin_education_republican_knowledge_1 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
					doctrine:doctrine_sin_education_republican_knowledge_3 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
				}
			}
		}
		traits = {
			sins = {
				education_republican_knowledge_2 = { scale = 1 weight = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

				text = doctrine_incompatible_strong_sin_trigger
				NOT = { doctrine:doctrine_sin_education_martial_prowess_2_strong = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines } }

			}

						doctrine:doctrine_sin_diplomatic_court_1_strong = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
						doctrine:doctrine_sin_diplomatic_court_strong = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }

					NOT = { doctrine:doctrine_virtue_scholarly_court_2 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines } }
					doctrine:doctrine_virtue_scholarly_court_2_strong = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
				}
			}
			custom_description = {
				text = doctrine_requires_sin_trigger

					doctrine:doctrine_sin_scholarly_court = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
				AND = {
						doctrine:doctrine_sin_scholarly_court_1 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
						doctrine:doctrine_sin_scholarly_court_2 = { is_in_list = selected_doctrines }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		traits = {

				scholarly_court = { scale = 2 weight = 4 }
			}
		}
